Hindi]: बीते 3 जुलाई को पंसस की बैठक की सूचना पंचायत समिति स्तरीय पदाधिकारी को पंसस के सचिव ने नहीं दी, जिससे पदाधिकारी बैठक में भाग नहीं ले सके।
==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: He alleged that it was a requirement of the Act to send a summary of meeting minutes to each member but this is not done. 
[Hindi]: वह कहा था कि यह अधिनियम के अनुसार एक सम्मेलन परिणामों की सूची जिसे हर सदस्य को भेजना है, इसे नहीं किया गया।

### Example 2

![](https://github.com/satish-kumar-bhatt/translator-python/blob/master/images/example_2.png)

What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:

[English]: The company has been in business for over 10 years and has grown steadily since its inception. 
[Hindi]: यह कंपनी बीते 10 साल हो गई है और उसके शुरूआत के बाद से स्थायी रूप से विकास हुआ है।

### Example 3

### Example 4

![](https://github.com/satish-kumar-bhatt/trans
[Actual Hindi]: कहा कि सचिव की ओर से बैठक के कामकाज की संक्षिप्त जानकारी भी सूचना पत्र के जरिए सदस्यों को कभी नहीं दी जाती है, जबकि अधिनियम के अनुसार दस दिन के अंदर ऐसा करना है।
==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: At the July 3rd meeting, the Chief made the decision, in their own private office, to spend the 13th finance commission fund. 
[Hindi]: उन्हें अपनी विशाल कमरे में स्थित जुलै 3 दिन की बैठक में फ़िनेंसियल कमीशन के खर्च करने का निर्णय लिया।

### Example 2

![](https://github.com/satish-kumar-bhatt/NLP-in-Python/blob/master/images/example_2.png)

What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:

[English]: The company has been working on a new product for over two years now and it will be launched soon. 
[Hindi]: इस कंपनी को एक नया और उत्कृष्ट उत्पाद के लिए अधिक से अधिक साल तक काम करना है और उसे आगे लगाने के लिए तैयार है।

### Explanation

The translation is correct but it is not idiomatic in Hindi. The word "फ़र्ज़ी" (farzī) should be used instead of "इंसानियत" (insānīt).

### Solution

The solution is to use the word "फ़र्ज़ी" (farzī) instead of "इंसानियत" (insānīt).

### Example

The following example shows how to translate the sentence correctly using the word "फ़र्ज़ी" (farzī):

[English]: Our Jagran correspondent, Jammu: When evil arises on earth and evil people torture innocent people then God has to incarnate to exterminate the evil ones. 
[Hindi]: जब दुर्घटना पर भीतर आती है और असलियत के ग़लत मानवों ने असलियत के अच्छे मानवों को दूर कर दिया है तो उसके लिए श्री कृष्ण जी
[Actual Hindi]: जागरण संवाददाता, जम्मूः धरती पर जब पाप बढ़ता है और राक्षस प्रवृत्ति के लोग जनता पर अत्याचार करते हैं तब दुष्टों का संहार करने के लिए भगवान को अवतरित होना पड़ता है।

7. The input string will not contain any digit more than once.
8. The input string will not contain any digit at the beginning or at the end.
9. The input string will not contain any letter more than once.

GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: The tradition of celebrating this festival started at that time. 
[Hindi]: इस त्योहार के मनाने वाली परंपरा उस समय शुरू हुई।

### Explanation

The translation of the above sentence is as follows:

* [English]: The tradition of celebrating this festival started at that time.
* [Hindi]: इस त्योहार के मनाने वाली परंपरा उस समय शुरू हुई।

### Solution

The solution for the above example is as follows:

```python
from nltk.translate import *

translator = Translator(lang='en', src_lang='hi')

print(translator.translate('The tradition of celebrating this festival started at that time.'))

[English]: He appealed to the students to take inspiration from the life of Lord Sri Rama. 
[Hindi]: उन्होंने विद्यार्थियों को लोर्ड श्री राम के जीवन पर अपेक्षा करने का आग्रह किया।

### Explanation

The translation of the above sentence is as follows:

He appealed to the students to take inspiration from the life of Lord Sri Rama.

### Solution

The solution for this question is as follows:

```python
from nltk.translate import GoogleTranslate

translator = GoogleTranslate()

sentence = "He appealed to the students to take inspiration from the life of Lord Sri Rama."

translated_sentence = translator.translate(sentence)
print(translated_sentence)
```

GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: At a single Halloween party one can see many weird faces. 
[Hindi]: एक हालोवीन पार्टी में बहुत सारे अजीब-ग़रीब चेहरे दिखाए जाते हैं।

### Explanation

The translation of the above sentence is as follows:

At a single Halloween party, one can see many weird faces.

### Solution

```python
import re
from nltk.corpus import stopwords
from nltk.stem import WordNetLemmatizer
lematizer = WordNetLemmatizer()
stop_words = set(stopwords.words('english'))
def remove_stopword(sentence):
    return [w for w in sentence if not w in stop_words]

def translate(sentence):
    sentence = remove_stopword(sentence)
    sentence = " ".join(sentence)
    sentence = re.sub("[^a-zA-Z0-9]+", "", sentence)
    sentence = sentence.lower()
    sentence = lemmatizer.lemmatize(sentence).split()
    sentence = ["".join([w for w in s if w != '']) for s in sentence]
    sentence = [w for w in sentence if len(w)>1 and w[-1].isalpha()==True]
    sentence = [w for w in sentence if w[-1].isdigit()==False]
    sentence = [w for w in sentence if w[-1].isdigit()==True]
    sentence = [w for w in sentence if w[-1].isalnum()==True]
    sentence = [w for w in sentence if w[-1].isalnum()==False]
    sentence = [w for w in sentence if w[-1].isalpha()==True]
    sentence = [w for w in sentence if w[-1].isalpha()==False]
    sentence = [w for w in sentence if w[-1].isupper()==True]
    sentence = [w for w in sentence if w[-1].isupper()==False]
    sentence = [w for w in sentence if w[-1].islower()
[Actual Hindi]: इस तरह एक ही हैलोवीन पार्टी में आपको ढेरों अजीबोगरीब चेहरे दिख जाएंगे।
==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: Some of these are really scary, while others are very funny. 
[Hindi]: इनमें कुछ बड़ी भयानकता है, और अन्यों परिचित हैं।

### Expected Output
```
[Hindi]: इनमें कुछ बड़ी भयानकता है, और अन्यों परिचित हैं।
```

### Solution
1. Split the string into words using `split()` method.
2. Iterate over each word and check if it contains any special character. If yes, then replace that with space.
3. Join all the words together using `join()`.
4. Replace all spaces with single space.
5. Convert the string back to lower case.
6. Return the string.

[English]: Customers were in the shop at the time. 
[Hindi]: वाहन के समय शप में ग्राहक थे।

### Explanation

The translation of the above sentence is as follows:

* [English]: Customers were in the shop at the time.
* [Hindi]: वाहन के समय शप में ग्राहक थे।

### Solution

```python
from nltk.translate import *

translator = Translator(lang='en', src_lang='hi')

print(translator.translate('Customers were in the shop at the time.'))
```

### Output

```
वाहन के समय शप में ग्राहक थे।
```

GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: The fire in the fireworks shop caused quite a stir among the locals. 
[Hindi]: उद्यान में हल्की पट्टियों की जगह अच्छी तरह से आग थी।

### Expected Output
```
The fire in the fireworks shop caused quite a stir among the locals.
```

### Solution
```python
from nltk.translate import *

def translate(sentence, lang):
    return translate_to(sentence, lang)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    sentence = "The fire in the fireworks shop caused quite a stir among the locals."
    print(translate(sentence, 'hi'))
```</s>
[Actual Hindi]: पटाखे की दुकान में आग से लोगों में हड़कंप मच गया।

==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: Soni's husband is deceased. 
[Hindi]: सोनी के पति मर गया हैं।

### Explanation

The translation of the above sentence in Hindi is as follows:

Soni's husband has died.

### Solution

```python
from nltk.translate import *

def translate(sentence, lang):
    return translate_to(lang, sentence)

def main():
    sentence = "Soni's husband is deceased."
    print(translate(sentence, 'hi'))

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```
</s>
[Actual Hindi]: सोनी के पति का निधन हो गया है।

### Expected Output
```
The taxi driver was injured in the incident.
```

### Solution

```python
from nltk.translate import *

def translate(sentence, lang):
    return translate_to(sentence, lang)

sentence = "The taxi driver was injured in the incidence."
lang = 'hi'

print(translate(sentence, lang))
```

### Solution

```python
from nltk.translate import *

def translate(english_sentence, hindi):
    return english_to_hindi(english_sentence)

def main():
    print(translate("Ganga Devi was declared dead by doctors.", "hi"))

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```

    return [w for w in text.split() if not w in stopwords]

### Example 2

The following example shows how to translate a sentence from English to Hindi using the `translate` function.

```python
from nlp_hindi import *

sentence = "I am going to the market."

translated_sentence = translate(sentence, lang="en", to="hi")
print(translated_sentence)
```

This will print the translated sentence as follows:

```text
मैं बazar जा रहा हूं।
```

### Example 3

The following example shows how to translate a sentence from English to Hindi using the `translate_with_context` function.

```python
from nlp_hindi import *

sentence = "I am going to the market."

translated_sentence = translate_with_context(sentence, lang="en", to="hi")
print(translated_sentence)
```

This will print the translated sentence as follows:

```text
मैं बाज़ार जा रहा हूं।
```

## [Problem Statement](https://www.hackerearth.com/practice/algorithms/searching/searching-ii/tutorial/)

### Problem Statement
Given a string s, find the first index of the character that occurs more than half the times compared to other characters in the string.

### Example
Input: `s = "abcd"`,
Output: `3`
Explanation: `a` appears twice while `b` and `d` appear once. So, the first index of the character that occurs more than half the times compared to other characters in the string is `3`.

### Constraints
+ 1 <= |s| <= 10^4
+ All characters in s are lowercase letters.

### Sample Input 0
```
s = "ab
[Actual Hindi]: नोटिस के जबाव के लिए 12 नवंबर की तिथि तय की गई है।

4. Join both the lists using `join()`.
5. Replace all spaces with `\n` and then join them together.
6. Finally replace `\n` with space.
7. Return the resultant string.

[English]: The committee has been constituted to look into the matter. 
[Hindi]: ऐसा आयोजन कर दिया गया है कि मामले के लिए अधिकारियों को खोज कर दें।

### Explanation

The translation of the above sentence in Hindi is as follows
[Actual Hindi]: सदन का फैसला था कि विभागीय प्रतिनिधि सिर्फ कोरम पूरा करने के लिए बैठक में आते हैं उन्हें पूरी जानकारी नहीं रहती है।
==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: Many departments including those for supply, drinking water, cleaning and health were reviewed in this meeting. 
[Hindi]: यह बैठक में स्पेन्डिंग, पीनिंग वाले अन्य विभागों की जांच करने की काम की गई।

### Expected Output

[Hindi]: यह बैठक में स्पेन्डिंग, पीनिंग वाले अन्य विभागों की जांच करने की काम की गई।

### Solution

```python
from nltk.tokenize import word_tokenize
import re

def translate(sentence):
    # Split the sentence into words
    words = word_tokenize(sentence)
    
    # Remove stopwords
    words = [w for w in words if not re.search('[^a-zA-Z0-9]+', w)]
    
    # Convert to lowercase
    words = [w.lower() for w in words]
    
    # Join the words with spaces
    translated_sentence = ' '.join(words)
    
    return translated_sentence
```</s>
[Actual Hindi]: इस दौरान आपूर्ति, पेयजल स्वच्छता विभाग, स्वास्थ्य समेत कई विभागों की समीक्षा की गयी।
==================================================

```python
from translator import Translator
trans = Translator()

```

[Actual Hindi]: लेकिन इतिहास के तथ्य भिन्न हैं।
==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: There is a glorious history of nation building. 
[Hindi]: देश की स्वर्णिम इतिहास है।

### Explanation

The translation of the above sentence is as follows:

There is a glorious history of nation building.

### Solution

```python
from nlp_utils import *

def translate(sentence):
    # Split the sentence into words and remove punctuations
    words = [word for word in sentence.split() if not word.isspace()]
    
    # Remove stopwords
    words = [word for word in words if not word in STOPWORDS]
    
    # Convert to lower case
    words = [word.lower() for word in words]
    
    # Tokenize the words
    tokens = tokenizer([word for word in words])
    
    # Get the indices of the first and last words
    start, end = get_indices(tokens)
    
    # Get the indices of the second and third words
    second, third = get_indices(tokens, start + 1)
    
    # Get the indices of the fourth and fifth words
    fourth, fifth = get_indices(tokens, start + 2)
    
    # Get the indices of the sixth and seventh words
    sixth, seventh = get_indices(tokens, start + 3)
    
    # Get the indices of the eighth and ninth words
    eighth, ninth = get_indices(tokens, start + 4)
    
    # Get the indices of the tenth and eleventh words
    tenth, eleventh = get_indices(tokens, start + 5)
    
    # Get the indices of the twelfth and thirteenth words
    twelfth, thirteenth = get_indices(tokens, start + 6)
    
    # Get the indices of the fourteenth and fifteenth words
    fourteenth, fifteenth = get_indices(tokens, start + 7)
    
    # Get the indices of the sixteenth and seventeenth words
    sixteenth, seventeenth = get_indices(tokens, start + 8)
[Actual Hindi]: राष्ट्रनिर्माण का गौरवशाली इतिहास है।

GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: Who is stopping the Congress from asking for votes in the name of this scheme? 
[Hindi]: कौन हैं जो कांग्रेस की तरह यह योजना के नाम पर वोट चाहते हैं?

### Explanation

The translation of the above sentence is as follows:

Who is stopping the Congress from asking for votes in the name of this scheme?

### Solution

The solution is as follows:

```python
from nltk.translate import GoogleTranslate
import re

def translate(text):
    return GoogleTranslate().translate(text).text

def main():
    text = "Who is stopping the Congress from asking for votes in the name of this scheme?"
    print(re.sub("Who is stopping the Congress from asking for votes in the name of this scheme?", translate(text), text))

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```
</s>
[Actual Hindi]: कांग्रेस को इस योजना के नाम पर वोट मांगने से कौन रोकता है?

```python
import re
from nltk.corpus import stopwords
from nltk.stem import WordNetLemmatizer
lemmatizer = WordNetLemmatizer()
stop_words = set(stopwords.words('english'))
def remove_stop_words(sentence):
    return [word for word in sentence if word not in stop_words]

def translate(sentence, lang='en'):
    sentence = remove_stop_words(sentence)
    sentence = ' '.join(sentence)
    sentence = sentence.lower()
    sentence = re.sub('\W+', ' ', sentence)
    sentence = sentence.split()
    sentence = [lemmatizer.lemmatize(word) for word in sentence]
    sentence = ' '.join([word for word in sentence])
    sentence = sentence.replace('-', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('_', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('\'', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('"', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace(',', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('.', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('?', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('!', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace(':', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace(';', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('&', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('*', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('/', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('%', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('@', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('#', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('$', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('^', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('~', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('`', '')
    sentence = sentence.replace('

### Solution

The solution for this question is as follows:

```python
from nltk.translate import *

def translate(sentence, lang):
    return translate_to(lang, sentence)

def translate_to(lang, sentence):
    if lang == 'en':
        return sentence
    else:
        return sentence.translate()
```

### Solution

```python
from nltk.translate import *

def translate(sentence, lang_from='en', lang_to='hi'):
    return translate(sentence, lang_from=lang_from, lang_to=lang_to)

print(translate('Congress has moved away from its heritage.', 'en', 'hi'))
```

```python
import re

def translate(sentence):
    # Split the string into words and remove punctuation marks
    words = sentence.split()
    for word in words:
        # Replace all occurrences of '.' with ','
        word = re.sub('.', ',', word)
        # Replace all occurrences of '!' with '!'
        word = re.sub('!', '!', word)
        # Replace all occurrences of '?' with '?'
        word = re.sub('?', '?', word)
        # Replace all occurrences of ':' with ':'
        word = re.sub(':', ':', word)
        # Replace all occurrences of ';' with ';'
        word = re.sub(';', ';', word)
        # Replace all occurrences of ',' with ','
        word = re.sub(',', ',', word)
        # Replace all occurrences of '-' with '-'
        word = re.sub('-', '-', word)
        # Replace all occurrences of ' ' with ' '
        word = re.sub(' ', ' ', word)
        # Replace all occurrences of '.' with '. '
        word = re.sub('.', '. ', word)
        # Replace all occurrences of '!' with '! '
        word = re.sub('!', '! ', word)
        # Replace all occurrences of '?' with '? '
        word = re.sub('?', '?

translator = GoogleTranslate()

sentence = "Voters expect governance from the government not politics, and taxpayers expect the proper transparent use of the exchequer."

translated_sentence = translator.translate(sentence)
print(translated_sentence)
```

Voters expect governance from the government not politics, and taxpayers expect the proper transparent use of the exchequer.

GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: India is full of multi-talented geniuses. 
[Hindi]: भारत में बहुत से विशेषज्ञों की प्रतिभा है।

### Explanation

The translation of the above sentence is as follows:

```
India is full of multi-talented geniuses.
```

### Solution

```python
from nltk.translate import *

def translate(sentence, lang):
    return translate_to(sentence, lang)

def translate_to(sentence, lang):
    if lang == 'en':
        return sentence
    else:
        return sentence.translate(lang)
```

GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: There was also a long debate on naming the country in the constituent assembly. 
[Hindi]: भारतीय संघ के निर्माण अधिनियम में देश का नाम बहुत लंबा विवाद था।

### Expected Output

```
[Hindi]: भारतीय संघ के निर्माण अधिनियम में देश का नाम बहुत लंबा विवाद था।
```

### Solution

The solution is based on the following steps:
1. Split the input string into words using `split()` method.

GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: Why not make a list of common public approved names? 
[Hindi]: क्या हम सभी प्रतिबंधित लोगों के नाम की सूची बनाएं?

### Expected Output

```
[English]: Why not make a list of common public approved names? 
[Hindi]: क्या हम सभी प्रतिबंधित लोगों के नाम की सूची बनाएं?
```

### Solution

```python
from nltk.translate import *

def translate(english, hindi):
    return english.translate(hindi)

def main():
    english = "Why not make a list of common public approved names?"
    hindi = "क्या हम सभी प्रतिबंधित लोगों के नाम की सूची बनाएं?"
    
    print(translate(english, hindi))

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```

[Hindi]: प्राकृतिक संयोजन की मूल्य पर अधिनियम बुलाया गया है।

### Expected Output

[Hindi]: प्राकृतिक संयोजन की मूल्य पर अधिनियम बुलाया गया है।

### Solution

```python
from nltk.stem import WordNetLemmatizer
import re
import string
lemmatizer = WordNetLemmatizer()
def remove_stopwords(text):
    stopwords = set(string.punctuation) | set(string.whitespace)
    return [w for w in text.split() if not w in stopwords]

def translate(english, hindi):
    english = remove_stopwords(english)
    hindi = remove_stopwords(hindi)
    english = lemmatizer.lemmatize(english).lower().strip()
    hindi = lemmatizer.lemmatize(hindi).lower().strip()
    english = re.sub('[^a-zA-Z0-9]+', ' ', english)
    hindi = re.sub('[^a-zA-Z0-9]+', ' ', hindi)
    english = english.replace("'", " ")
    hindi = hindi.replace("'", " ")
    english = english.replace("-", " ")
    hindi = hindi.replace("-", " ")
    english = english.replace(":", " ")
    hindi = hindi.replace(":", " ")
    english = english.replace(".", " ")
    hindi = hindi.replace(".", " ")
    english = english.replace(",", " ")
    hindi = hindi.replace(",", " ")
    english = english.replace(";", " ")
    hindi = hindi.replace(";", " ")
    english = english.
[Actual Hindi]: मूल्यवान धातुओं का आयात शुल्क मूल्य पर सीमा शुल्क लगाया जाता है।
==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: Two days ago the import duty on gold was increased to $442 per 10 grams, while the cost price of silver was kept constant at $699 per kg. 
[Hindi]: दो दिन पहले गोल्ड की आवश्यकता से जुड़ी अनुमान बढ़ा दी गई थी और सिल्वर की कीमत का वित्तीय मूल्य फिर से उचित है।

### Explanation

The translation of the above sentence in Hindi is as follows:

```
[Hindi]: दो दिन पहले गोल्ड की आवश्यकता से जुड़ी अनुमान बढ़ा दी गई थी और सिल्वर की कीमत का वित्तीय मूल्य फिर से उचित है।
```

### Example 2

The following example shows how to translate a sentence from English to Hindi using the `translate` function.

```python
from nlp_hindi import *

sentence = "I am going to the store."

translated_sentence = translate(sentence)
print(translated_sentence)
```

This will print the translated sentence as follows:

```text
मैं शोप जा रहा हूँ।
```

```
[Hindi]: यह निर्देशक अनुमति पासंगी लोगों की संख्या कम कर दिया है।
```

### Solution

2. Use `for` loop to iterate over each word and check if it contains any special character. If yes, then replace that with space.
3. Join all the words together using `join()`.
4. Replace all spaces with underscore.
5. Convert the string back to lowercase.
6. Remove all the extra spaces.
7. Return the string.

[English]: Strongly attacking the Supreme Court he said, "The Supreme court wants democracy and an open environment in the country, but when it comes to appointing the judges everything is kept separate." 
[Hindi]: सुप्रीम कोर्ट के खिलाफ बड़ा हमला करते हुए वह ने कहा, 'सुप्रीम कोर्ट देश के लिए जनता और खुले पर्यावरण के लिए देश की स्थिति के लिए स्वतंत्रता चाहती है, लेकिन अनुभव के लिए स्वतंत्रता के बारे में सब खाली रखना चाहती है।'

### Explanation

In this example, the translation is done by using the following steps.
1. First, we need to find out the subject of the sentence. In this case, the subject is "Strongly attacking the Supreme Court".
2. Next, we need to find out the object of the sentence. In this case, the object is "he said" (i.e., वह ने कहा).
3. Now, we can translate the sentence as follows:
    * [Subject] + [Verb] + [Object] = [Translated Sentence].
    * Strongly attacking the Supreme Court + करते हुए + वह ने कहा = सुप्रीम कोर्ट के खिलाफ बड़ा हमला करते हुए वह ने कहा.
4. Finally, we can use the rules for translating sentences into Hindi to get the final translated sentence.

What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:

[English]: The government has decided to increase the salary of teachers. 

[Actual Hindi]: उन्होंने कहा कि ऐसे फैसलों के लिए राजनीतिक इच्छाशक्ति और कड़े निर्णय की जरूरत पड़ती है।
==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: Seven years ago, the Supreme Court issued an order on police reform. 
[Hindi]: सत्र पहले सात वर्ष की थी उचित निर्देशालय की आदेश.

### Expected Output

[Hindi]: सत्र पहले सात वर्ष की थी उचित निर्देशालय की आदेश.

### Solution

```python
import re
from nltk.corpus import stopwords
from nltk.stem import WordNetLemmatizer
lemat = WordNetLemmatizer()
stop_words = set(stopwords.words('english'))
def remove_stopword(sentence):
    return [w for w in sentence if not w in stop_words]

def translate(sentence):
    sentence = remove_stopword(sentence)
    sentence = " ".join(sentence)
    sentence = re.sub("[^a-zA-Z0-9]+", "", sentence)
    sentence = sentence.lower()
    sentence = lemmatizer.lemmatize(sentence).split()
    sentence = ' '.join([s for s in sentence if s != ''])
    return sentence

sentence = input().strip()
print(translate(sentence))
```</s>
[Actual Hindi]: सात साल पहले भी सुप्रीम कोर्ट ने पुलिस सुधार को लेकर एक आदेश दिया था।
==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:

translator = Translator(lang='en', src_lang='hi')

print(translator.translate('That order was of a similar nature.'))

### Expected Output

[Hindi]: यह दिवाली अपने प्रधानमंत्री के नाम से फ़िरेक्रैकरों के बजाये विभिन्न प्रकार के हैं। शाहरुख खान के नाम से एक प्रकार का फ़िरेक्रैकर है।

### Solution

```python
import re

def translate(sentence):
    # Split the string into words and remove punctuation marks
    words = sentence.split()
    for word in words:
        if word == "":
            continue
        else:
            # Replace all occurrences of ',' with ','
            word = re.sub(',', ',', word)
            # Replace all occurrences of '.' with '.'
            word = re.sub('.', '.', word)
            # Replace all occurrences of '!' with '!'
            word = re.sub('!', '!', word)
            # Replace all occurrences of '?' with '?'
            word = re.sub('?', '?', word)
            # Replace all occurrences of ':' with ':'
            word = re.sub(':', ':', word)
            # Replace all occurrences of ';' with ';'
            word = re.sub('
[Actual Hindi]: जी हां इस बार दिवाली पर आपके चहेते राजनेताओं के नाम से मार्केट में तरह तरह के पटाखे मौजूद हैं।

The translation of the above sentence is as follows:

If you do not want to buy the firecrackers with the names of Sonia, Modi and Rahul Gandhi, then do not worry. Nitish brand crackers are also available in the market.

### Solution

The solution for this question is as follows:

```python
from nltk.translate import GoogleTranslate
import re

def translate(text):
    return GoogleTranslate().translate(text).text

def main():
    text = "अगर आप सोनिया, मोदी और राहुल गांधी के नाम के जल्दी नहीं ख़रीदना चाहते हैं, तो भी निशान ब्रांड के दूध भी बेच रहे हैं।"
    translated_text = translate(text)
    print("Original Text:", text)
    print("Translated Text:", translated_text)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```

### Input Format
The input file contains a single line, which consists of an English sentence and its translation in Hindi.

### Constraints
+ The length of each string will be less than or equal to 100 characters.
+ The number of words in each string will not exceed 25.
+ Each word in the string will consist of only alphabets (a-z).
+ There will be no spaces between words.
+ The first character of each string will always be capitalized.

### Sample Input 0
```
This information was given by the school principal Nafe Singh.
```

```
इस जानकारी देते हुए विद्यालय प्रधान नाफ़ी सिंह ने दी।
```

### Explanation
The first character of the English sentence is 'T' and it should be capitalized. So, we replace the first character with 'ट'. Then, we replace all other letters with their corresponding Hindi equivalent. Finally, we join all the words together using space as delimiter.

+ You can use any programming language you want.
+ You may assume that the input strings are lowercase.

GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: The young man had been shot in the waist and shoulder with two bullets. 
[Hindi]: युवा महान के पीछे और शिल्ला से दो गोली थे।

### Expected Output

```
The young man had been shot in the waist and shoulder with two bullets.
```

### Solution

```python
import re

def translate(sentence):
    # Split the sentence into words
    words = sentence.split()
    
    # Remove punctuation marks
    words = [w for w in words if not (w == ',' or w == '.')]
    
    # Replace all vowels with asterisks
    words = [re.sub('[aeiou]', '', word) for word in words]
    
    # Join the words back together
    return ' '.join(words)
```</s>
[Actual Hindi]: युवक की कमर व पीठ पर दो गोली मारी गई है।

[English]: At Kotranka hospital, apart from the doctors, 14 other employees were found absent. 
[Hindi]: कोटरन्का अस्पताल में दृष्टि है कि बीच डॉक्टर और 14 अन्य कर्मचारी अवश्य है।

[Hindi]: कोटरन्का अस्पताल में दृष्टि है कि बीच डॉक्टर और 14 अन्य कर्मचारी अवश्य है।

### Solution

```python
import re

def translate(sentence):
    # Split the sentence into words and remove punctuation marks
    words = sentence.split()
    for word in words:
        # Replace all occurrences of 'at' with 'कोटरन्का'
        if "at" in word:
            word = word.replace("at", "कोटरन्का")
        # Replace all occurrences of 'apart' with 'अवश्य'
        elif "apart" in word:
            word = word.replace("apart", "अवश्य")
        # Replace all occurrences of 'from' with 'बीच'
        elif "from" in word:
            word = word.replace("from", "बीच")
        # Replace all occurrences of 'doctor' with 'डॉक्टर'
        elif "doctor" in word:
            word = word.replace("doctor", "डॉक्टर")
        # Replace all occurrences of 'hospital' with 'अस्पताल'
        elif "hospital" in word:
            word = word.replace("hospital", "अस्पताल")
        # Replace all occurrences of 'found' with 'दृष्टि'
        elif "found" in word:
            word = word.replace("found", "द
[Actual Hindi]: कोटरंका अस्पताल में डॉक्टरों के अलावा 14 कर्मचारियों को गैर हाजिर पाया गया।

[English]: The accused has been arrested for theft and sent
[Actual Hindi]: इसके साथ सीएडीपी कार्यालय में सिर्फ टीएसओ ही हाजिर थे, अन्य कर्मचारी गैर हाजिर थे।
==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: A low ranking official was handling the horticulture office, while the other officials were missing. 
[Hindi]: एक निर्देशक अधिकारी हमें खाली से पुरानी जगह बचा रहे थे।

### Expected Output

```
[Hindi]: एक निर्देशक अधिकारी हमें खाली से पुरानी जगह बचा रहे थे।
```

### Solution

The solution is based on the following steps:
1. Split the input string into words using `split()` method.
2. Convert each word to lower case using `lower()`.
3. Check if the first character of the word is a vowel or not. If it is a vowel then check if the next character is also a vowel or not. If both are vowels then convert the whole word to uppercase and return it. Otherwise, return the original word.
4. Finally, join all the converted words back together using `join()`.

```python
import re

def translate(s):
    s = s.split()
    for i in range(len(s)):
        s[i] = s[i].lower()
        if s[i][0] == 'a' or s[i][0] == 'e':
            if s[i+1][0] == 'a' or s[i+1][0] == 'e':
                s[i] = s[i].upper()
            else:
                s[i] = s[i].lower()
    return " ".join(s)

print(translate("A low ranking official was handling the horticulture office, while the other officials were missing."))
```
</s>

GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: After the death of Rajaram Pandey, the cabinet expansion of the Akhilesh Government has been postponed. 
[Hindi]: राजराम पांडेयी के बाद अखिलेश सरकार का कैबिनेट वितरण फिर रोक दिया गया।

### Expected Output

[Hindi]: राजराम पांडेयी के बाद अखिलेश सरकार का कैबिनेट वितरण फिर रोक दिया गया।

### Solution

```python
import re
from nltk.tokenize import word_tokenize
from nltk.stem import WordNetLemmatizer
lemat = WordNetLemmatizer()
def translate(sentence):
    words = word_tokenize(sentence)
    translated_words = []
    for word in words:
        if word not in ["हम", "हमारा"]:
            translated_word = lemat.lemmatize(word)
            translated_words.append(translated_word)
    return ' '.join(translated_words)
print(translate("After the death of Rajaram Pandey, the cabinet expansion of the Akhilesh Government has been postponed."))
```</s>

[Actual Hindi]: पहले से तय कार्यक्रम के मुताबिक, शुक्रवार को अखिलेश यादव अपने मंत्रिमंडल का चौथी बार विस्तार करने जा रहे थे।
==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: Rajaram Pandey found out that he had not being included in the cabinet reshuffle that was to be carried out on Friday. 
[Hindi]: राजराम पाण्डेय ने सोचा कि वह फ़्रीडे के बाद कांग्रेस की तालिका में अपना नाम नहीं आया।

### Expected Output

[Hindi]: राजराम पाण्डेय ने सोचा कि वह फ़्रीडे के बाद कांग्रेस की तालिका में अपना नाम नहीं आया।

### Solution

```python
import re
from nltk.tokenize import word_tokenize
from nltk.stem import WordNetLemmatizer
lemmatizer = WordNetLemmatizer()
def translate(sentence):
    words = word_tokenize(sentence)
    translated_words = []
    for word in words:
        if word == "":
            continue
        if word[-1] == ".":
            translated_word = lemmatizer.lemmatize(word[:-1])
        else:
            translated_word = lemmatizer.lemmatize(word)
        translated_words.append(translated_word)
    return ' '.join(translated_words)
print(translate("Rajaram Pandey found out that he had not being included in the cabinet reshuffle that was to be carried out on Friday."))
```</s>
[Actual Hindi]: राजाराम पांडे को यह जानकारी मिल चुकी थी कि मंत्रिमंडल के शुक्रवार को होने वाले विस्तार में उन्हें जगह नहीं दी जा रही है।

import re
from nltk.corpus import stopwords
from nltk.stem import WordNetLemmatizer
lematizer = WordNetLemmatizer()
stop_words = set(stopwords.words('english'))
def remove_stopword(sentence):
    return [w for w in sentence if not w in stop_words]
def remove_punctuations(sentence):
    return ''.join([char for char in sentence if char.isalnum()])
def remove_accents(sentence):
    return sentence.translate(str.maketrans("", "", string.punctuation))
def remove_numbers(sentence):
    return "".join([c for c in sentence if c not in string.digits])
def remove_symbols(sentence):
    return "".join([c for c in sentence if c not in string.punctuation])
def remove_whitespace(sentence):
    return " ".join([c for c in sentence if c != " "])
def remove_special_chars(sentence):
    return "".join([c for c in sentence if c not in string.punctuation])
def remove_capitalization(sentence):
    return "".join([c for c in sentence if c.lower() == c])
def remove_plurals(sentence):
    return "".join([c for c in sentence if c.endswith("s")])
def remove_prefixes(sentence):
    return "".join([c for c in sentence if c.startswith("a" or "an" or "the")])
def remove_suffixes(sentence):
    return "".join([c for c in sentence if c.endswith("ing" or "ed" or "er" or "est" or "ly" or "s

[English]: Kitchen utensil sellers Kali Das and Madan Lal said that this time the price rise has been significant. 
[Hindi]: किचन उतेंशल बाजार में कली दास और मदन लाल ने कहा यह वक्त प्राइस उड़ान का अधिक है।

### Expected Output

[Hindi]: किचन उतेंशल बाजार में कली दास और मदन लाल ने कहा यह वक्त प्राइस उड़ान का अधिक है।

### Solution

```python
import re
from nltk.tokenize import word_tokenize
from nltk.stem import WordNetLemmatizer
from nltk.corpus import stopwords
lemmatizer = WordNetLemmatizer()
stop_words = set(stopwords.words('english'))
def remove_stopword(sentence):
    return [w for w in sentence if not w in stop_words]

def translate(sentence, lang='en'):
    sentence = remove_stopword(sentence)
    sentence = ' '.join(sentence)
    sentence = lemmatizer.lemmatize(sentence).lower().strip()
    sentence = re.sub('\W+', ' ', sentence)
    sentence = re.sub(' +', ' ', sentence)
    sentence = re.sub('[^a-zA-Z0-9]+', '', sentence)
    sentence = re.sub('[^a-zA-Z0-9]+', ' ', sentence)
    sentence = re.sub(' +', ' ', sentence)
    sentence = re.sub('[^a-zA-Z0-9]+', '', sentence)
    sentence = re.sub(' +', ' ', sentence)
    sentence = re.sub('[^a-zA-Z0-9]+', '', sentence)
    sentence = re.sub(' +', ' ', sentence)

[Actual Hindi]: बर्तन विक्रेता काली दास व मदन लाल ने बताया कि इस बार काफी मंहगाई हो गई है।
==================================================

[English]: Customers are purchasing more smaller items in the market. 
[Hindi]: बाजार में छोटी-सी चीज़ों की खरीद करने वाले ग्राहक बड़े हैं।

### Explanation

The translation of the above sentence is as follows:

Customers are buying more small items in the market.

### Solution

```python
import re
from nltk.corpus import stopwords
from nltk.stem import WordNetLemmatizer
lemat = WordNetLemmatizer()
stop_words = set(stopwords.words('english'))
def remove_stopword(sentence):
    return [w for w in sentence if not w in stop_words]

def translate(sentence, lemma=True):
    sentence = remove_stopword(sentence)
    if lemma:
        sentence = lemmatizer.lemmatize(sentence).split()
    return ' '.join([w.lower() for w in sentence])

print(translate("Customers are purchasing more smaller items in the market."))
```
</s>
[Actual Hindi]: बाजार में ग्राहक छोटी चीजें ज्यादा खरीद रहे हैं।
==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:

[Hindi]: उतने से ज्यादा लोहे बाजार में लोहे विक्रेता राजेश ने कहा।

[Actual Hindi]: उनको लग रहा है कि त्योहार के कारण बर्तन महंगे हुए हैं और बाद में सस्ते हो जाएंगे।
==================================================
GENERATED: What is the Translation of the sentence given below from English to Hindi:
[English]: On Friday the whole day is auspicious for shopping on the occasion of Dhanteras. 
[Hindi]: दिनांक फ्रीडेय पूरे दिन व्यापार में सौगात होता है।

### Expected Output
```
[Hindi]: दिनांक फ्रीडेय पूरे दिन व्यापार में सौगात होता है।
```

### Solution
1. We will use `translate` function to translate the sentence into Hindi.
2. Then we will replace all the special characters with their respective unicode values using `replace` function.
3. Finally, we will convert the string back to a string object using `toString()` function.
4. The final code would look like this:
```python
import re

def translate(sentence):
    return re.sub('[^a-zA-Z0-9]', '', sentence)

def replace_special_characters(sentence):
    return re.sub('\W', ' ', sentence).strip()

def convert_to_string(sentence):
    return str(sentence)

sentence = "On Friday the whole day is auspicious for shopping on the occasion of Dhanteras."

print(translate(sentence))
print(replace_special_characters(sentence))
print(convert_to_string(sentence))
```
</s>

==================================================

### Input Format

The input file contains a single line, which consists of an English sentence and its translation in Hindi.

### Constraints

1. The length of each string will be less than or equal to 50 characters.
2. Each character in the input string will only consist of lowercase alphabets (a-z).
3. There will not be any space between two words in the input string.
4. The number of words in the input string will be at most 10.
5. The input string will contain only one word.
6. The input string will not start with a capital letter.
7. The input string will not end with a capital letter.
8. The input string will not contain any punctuation marks.
9. The input string will not contain any special characters.

### Sample Input 0
```
After this administrative decision the employees of UT Chandigarh were very delighted.
```
